  <script>
   function getQueryParam(paramName) {
        var query = window.location.search.substring(1);
        var params = query.split('&');
        for (var i = 0; i < params.length; i += 1) {
          var pair = params[i].split('=');
          if (pair[0] === paramName) {
            return pair[1];
          }
        }
        return false;
      };
      function removeURLParameter(url, param) {
        var urlParts = url.split('?');
        if (urlParts.length >= 2) {
          var prefix = "".concat(encodeURIComponent(param), "=");
          var params = urlParts[1].split(/[&;]/g);
          for (var i = params.length - 1; i >= 0; i -= 1) {
            if (params[i].lastIndexOf(prefix, 0) !== -1) {
              params.splice(i, 1);
            }
          }
          url = urlParts[0];
          if (params.length > 0) {
            url += "?".concat(params.join('&'));
          }
          return url;
        }
        return url;
      };
      function setCookie(cookieName, value, daysToExpire) {
        var expires = '';
        if (daysToExpire) {
          var date = new Date();
          date.setTime(date.getTime() + daysToExpire * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
          expires = "; expires=".concat(date.toGMTString());
        }
        if (expires !== '') {
          document.cookie = "".concat(cookieName, "=").concat(value).concat(expires, "; path=/");
        }
        return true;
      };
      (function(){
        var hid = getQueryParam('hid');
        if (!hid) {
          return;
        }
        setCookie('hid', hid, 90);
        window.location.replace(removeURLParameter(window.location.href, 'hid'));
      })();
  </script>

   window.mdp = window.mdp || {};
      window.mdp.getCookieValue = function getCookieValue(name) {
        var cookie = document.cookie.match('(^|;)\\s*' + name + '\\s*=\\s*([^;]+)');
        return cookie ? decodeURIComponent(cookie.pop()) : '';
      }
  </script>

   <section class="component category-page-list-three-featured categoryPageListThreeFeatured" data-label-number="" data-tracking-zone="three-feature-block">
    <h2 class="categoryPageListThreeFeatured__title">
     <span>
      Mental Health
     </span>
    </h2>
    <div class="categoryPageListThreeFeatured__content">
     <div class="category-page-item ">

   <section class="component category-page-list-three-featured categoryPageListThreeFeatured" data-label-number="" data-tracking-zone="three-feature-block">
    <h2 class="categoryPageListThreeFeatured__title">
     <span>
      Working It Out
     </span>
    </h2>
    <div class="categoryPageListThreeFeatured__content">
     <div class="category-page-item ">
